1)
The Path of Restoration
Whenever any being begins its journey, it must take a certain path. Whether it goes east or west, or south or north, it will go, but the difference lies in whether it goes straight or in a winding manner. 
Four Principles for Walking the Path of Life
When we look at humanity, everyone desires to walk the path of life in a straight line. This must be the wish of all human beings. So what must be done to achieve this? There must be a purpose. If one does not set a standard that says, "I will go there," one cannot go straight. 
And when one sets a purpose, there can only be one path that is closest to that purpose. However, there can be various ways to reach that purpose, even if they are slightly curved; some may go this way, and some may go that way... There are many paths, it seems. 
Therefore, to go straight toward a certain goal, one must know the direction in which to go. First, one must establish a purpose. In other words, the direction is the issue. Next, the question is whether to go quickly or slowly. Then, whether the environment is comfortable or uncomfortable, good or bad becomes an issue. When going to the destination, one must not be swayed by direction, environment, or speed. If one is swayed by any of these, various results can occur on the way to the destination. 
Then, regarding who should take that path, it can be either oneself or someone else; these two types arise. 
However, when we say "our path," it means that I must go, not that I send someone else. Each person must go. 
Do you want to go far or close? "Far." How far? "Very far." A person who thinks of going a long way cannot be happy for a long time. Why? Because one cannot go without investment, sacrifice, and effort in the process of going. Yet, one still wants to go that long way? "Yes." So how many years will it take to reach that destination? 
When looking at an individual, if that individual clearly sets a distant goal and breaks through to that goal, that person will become someone who has succeeded in a way that no one else can follow. Even if they do not achieve the overall goal, there will be results in achieving partial goals along the way. 
The issue here is how much enthusiasm and effort I have. Do I have the will? To set a distant goal and go, there must be a desire for that goal, and a sense of purpose regarding that goal. Moreover, the desire must stimulate me daily. The desire must pull me forward. This applies to individuals as well as to nations and peoples. 
When we look at a nation, if that nation has an unchanging sense of purpose centered on going a long distance or for the happiness of all humanity, and continues to move forward, that nation will develop more than any other. 
When we see humans living on this earth, since they can only live for 70 or 80 years, the thought is generally that they want to achieve something within those 70 or 80 years. Isn't that so? The path one can take in a lifetime is only this much... No matter how hard one tries, one can only go a distance that can be covered in a lifetime. Even if one goes alone, it is at most... Therefore, humans desire to center themselves and have a significant impact on the whole, hoping for great results in a short time. That is what they long for. We know that this is human desire. 
What sense of purpose should one have?
Although the path of life is 70 or 80 years, if one becomes a central figure and establishes a sense of purpose that drives the whole, and if that purpose pushes the entire world toward it, the results will be vast. Therefore, to have a purpose that can positively influence the whole, it must be the highest sense of purpose. If that purpose is not only for oneself but also a purpose that humans in the past wanted, that all of humanity today wants, and that future people will also want, then if it is presented clearly and explained once, and if the results are shown to be good, humanity will inevitably seek that purpose. Isn't that so? "Yes." 
Therefore, we must understand that today, humanity needs a clear, true destination and purpose for life that humanity must reach throughout the past, present, and future. Thus, the question is what sense of purpose humanity will carry as it moves forward. 
However, there is no sense of purpose. Consider where one places their purpose. Some place it on studying. Some place it on a loved one, or on family, that is, the home. Others place it on their job. Some, at most, place their purpose on their country. Therefore, when you think about yourselves, it is the most important issue where you place your sense of purpose. 
That sense of purpose... It is because of that that I must live, I must eat, I must wear clothes, and I must make efforts. This conclusion arises. One must live in an inseparable relationship with that sense of purpose. It must be definitive. Otherwise, one cannot accelerate their speed. 
Moreover, one cannot pioneer the environment. 
So this morning, we must think about where we placed our purpose during the past year of 1973. Therefore, we need to reflect once again. 
Then, where do you want to place your sense of purpose? Do you want to place it on the individual? "No." It is undeniable that you want to place it on the family rather than the individual. So do you want to place it only on the family? You said you want to place it on something distant... Therefore, you want to place it on the tribe rather than the family. Do you want to place it only on the tribe? Then you want to place it on the country, on the world. 
In other words, the family is larger than the individual, right? So you want to place it on the family. And you want to place it on the tribe, which is larger than the family, and then on the country, and on the world. Will that be the end? No. There is something larger... In the context of the Unification Church, it is the Heavenly Parent, the Heavenly Parent. So does that end there? "No." There is God who governs this. Do you understand? God is the center of everything. If there is such a God, if there is a deity, we must inevitably place our purpose on God. This is the ultimate conclusion. Is that true for you too? "Yes." 
The journey begins with the individual
Then, when placing the purpose on God, can one start by saying, "Ah, I must seek the universe"? No. So let’s think about what the shortest path to the universe is. Where should one start? "From the individual." The individual is the issue. 
Can the individual start arbitrarily? No. If there is God, the relationship between God and the individual is like a taut string... This is the purpose point, and this is the starting point. 
So where is the shortest path? No matter how wide it is, it starts from my individual. Then where is the purpose point my heart is heading toward? Where is that? It is my body. My body and mind must become one. Therefore, God commands our hearts to "Become one with the body for the sake of world restoration." 
If the heart and body are not united, the heart goes its own way, and the body goes its own way, wandering separately. Then one cannot go toward a single destination. A person who is inconsistent cannot succeed. Therefore, before you set out for a distant place, the first thing you must do is unite your body and mind. 
That is why the first step on the path we must take is the unification of body and mind. The heart goes through the path of the body. So where must we go? What is the direction? The closest direction is the family. One must understand that there are parents and children in the family. They must become one. This must become one. The partner must become one. 
This centers around me, with the parents' family above me and the children's family below me. If we break this down, it becomes male and female. And it becomes front and back, left and right. Therefore, this must also become one here, and this must also become one, and the four must become one. Thus, a person without a partner cannot be happy. Because we humans are the center of the universe, the relationship of up and down, front and back can only be established in the family. Is that so, or not? "Yes." 
In Western thought, individualism is in a dangerous position. "Where are the parents, where are the siblings, where are the spouse and children...?" This is how it comes out. They have lost everything. Also, "Where is my heart and body? The body does not need the heart, and the heart does not need the body." So where is the position? It is nonexistent. Therefore, it leads to destruction. It is currently in decline. Therefore, as you know, parents are absolutely necessary, and spouses and children are absolutely necessary. 
Now, can there be multiple parents? Is there anyone who desires that? "No." That is the same as saying there are two Gods. If one parent says to go this way and the other parent says to go that way, can one reach the destination? Also, can there be two partners? "No." If that happens, the center will waver. Can children waver? Can just anyone become a child? "No." 
Tradition must be respected
Parents are a straight line before their children, and children are a straight line before their parents. What does that mean? It is bloodline, bloodline. The bloodline must not waver. It must be passed down straight. It must be inherited as it has been passed down from ancestors. There may be thousands of generations, but if it is inherited straight from this starting point, how fast will it be? It will be straight. That will lead to great development. 
If there are ancestors here, what will happen? (Pointing while speaking) Will you inherit this or will you inherit that? In other words, if there is an ancestor going this way among the ancestors, then in terms of a straight line, it will only have advanced this much. It has gone like this. The distance is the same, but has this advanced? This is not advancement; rather, it is an obstruction. For this to advance, it must either go around or go back. (Pointing to what was written) 
That is why the saying that tradition must be respected holds true. Today, the Jews are moving the world and holding all the global economic power. The Jewish people boast the longest tradition in the world. That is why the Jews are currently an issue. However, if the Jews had become one with God, it would have been fine, but because they could not become one with God... If there is a king who respects tradition above all, that king is God. The Jews centered on God up to the standards of the individual, family, tribe, nation. However, they could not center on God at the global standard. Therefore, as we enter the global age, the Jews will decline. Thus, we must center on God and transition into the global age. 
The highest purpose of the Unification Church is the Heavenly Parent where heaven and earth meet.
Whether an individual is a person of character or not depends on whether the body and mind unite centered on order. Also, the rise and fall of the family depends on whether the family completely unites and aligns with the direction God is going, and the differences determine the rankings of first, second, and third. Depending on the distance, some families among the national citizens receive blessings, while others do not. You all know that, right? Those close to you are good, while those far away... God is the same. 
From this perspective, do you need parents? "Yes." Therefore, we must respect heaven. Parents are symbols of heaven. The command to absolutely obey the words of parents comes from here. 
Descendants are determined by their parents. Why? To fully receive the gifts left by the ancestors, one must become completely one with the parents. To become one with the parents, one must obey and submit to become one. This means one must always be united. 
In terms of male and female, if the right side is male, the left side is female. So who should start first? Should the woman start first, or should the man start first? "The man." The man must start first. What is the fall? The fall is when the woman started first. When looking at men and women on this earth, who is the center? It is not the woman; it is the man. Westerners talk about equality, but there is an order to equality. Women, do you have any complaints? "No." In American families, women seem to govern men, but such households will decline. The man has the subjectivity. However, women are inversely governing. The man may be governed, but internally he is dissatisfied. 
Women are the earth, the earth. Men are heaven. Therefore, men are protruding and...
The woman is concave, right? Because she is concave, she must receive. When water is poured, it must be received. Here, the women, don't think that the teacher teaches like that. The principles of heaven and earth are all like that. It cannot be denied. A woman must be obedient for the water to pool. Obedient women receive blessings.

Can you freely switch between women and men? If you switch, the center will be divided. If both the woman and the man become centers, they will be separated. That is why the Western customs today are wrong. They will perish.

Marriage must only happen once. Is there anyone who thinks they will definitely get divorced when they marry? If you get divorced, do you say you have failed or succeeded? "Failed." Failure is worse than not having done it at all. Such social issues are all...

In the end, the question is where you start from and where you go. I cannot go further without going through the family. You must understand that you cannot go into the realm of lineage without going through the family.

So I must enter the family. The more I enter the family and serve it, what do I become? I become a central being in the family. Thus, I should be filial to my parents, and become a model family united with my wife and children, so that everyone in the neighborhood praises us and wants to unite, right? It's the same. Then the relatives will want to unite with me. Should I say, "Hey, relatives, all serve me"? No, there is only the way of serving and respecting everyone.

God rises like this, and I rise like this. It's the same. (While writing on the board) I rise like this, I go like this, and then I rise like this again; I resemble God. I am like God. Then where is the highest point of contact? Here, in the family? Of course, there is contact in the family. However, the highest point of contact is here. (Pointing to what he wrote) Therefore, where do we center our contact? Where is the highest point of contact? It is at the intersection of heaven and earth. Isn't that right? It is the place where heaven and earth meet. Therefore, what is God's wish? It is to meet here. 

What is the wish of humanity? Humanity's wish is also to meet here. From this perspective, where does our Unification Church set its goal? It sets its goal at the place called the cosmos. Thus, it concludes that we have the highest purpose that has never existed in history.

Why is the principle of cosmic restoration necessary for us? To rise, there are individuals, tribes, nations, the world, and the cosmos. However, since the cosmos has not yet emerged, we must create it and rise. Therefore, for individuals to rise, they must stand within the family. They must enter the family. Then where does the family need to go? It must enter here. Otherwise, there is no way to go. So I am in the middle of this.

Individuals and families must unite and go together. Where does the tribe need to go? There is no other way. There is only this way, and to go this way, how must we proceed? We must go here. Therefore, there is no way other than to make everything one centered on the tribe. Is there another way to go like this? Is there another way? "No." In the end, the nation exists for the world. It is all the same.

What is the purpose of God's restoration providence? What is God's purpose? It is to save heaven and earth. It is to eliminate the hell of the earthly and heavenly worlds. What is our human purpose? It is to possess God. Has there been a historical era with such a purpose? "No."

Until now, people have centered on their own religions and claimed to be the best. Until now, everyone has said, "I believe and let's go to heaven." But when I went to the spirit world, I saw that such people... where is there a way to go?

Today is the first Sunday of this year. Since we gathered early, you might be tired, but please listen to these words. And if someone is dozing off, let them take the seat next to them and lie down to listen. (Laughter) If one-third of you doze off, I will only speak to that one-third. The teacher is speaking earnestly, but if you say, "I will sleep earnestly," that is Satan, isn't it?

You must not be unaware of this. The purpose of why the principle of cosmic restoration is necessary must be clear. You cannot have interest in it if you do not know how precious that value is. Therefore, you must understand how great this purpose is that we have in the historical era.

So God sends the Messiah to establish families and create this path... When this goes toward the highest purpose, the tribe and the nation grow together as one. When looking at this world, the nation is like the heart, so God always works in the heart and commands the body to be governed, just like if the Jews had completely united with Jesus, they would have ruled not only the Roman Empire but the entire world without any problem.

If the Messiah had united with them, it would have been so. Since the nation is in the position of the heart, it is not a problem of Rome. Because the Messiah is the center of the heart, when united with God, a powerful force is activated, allowing a person with the heart to govern the body, and thus the Roman Empire and the world would have been governed without any problem.

After the world becomes one, the spirit world, being the world of angels, is waiting and preparing for the Messiah to come to the physical world to unite. Therefore, the spirit world is not a problem. If the earthly world is resolved, the spirit world can unite immediately.

Think about it. Why can't the spirit world act freely in this era? Because God is the core of all existence, humans must be completely united with God. There must be a person whose heart and body are completely united. Only such a person can... Without moving people freely, the world cannot be moved. Why? Because the world is not united. Do you understand why? "Yes." The spirit world is like the world of angels. The angelic world is external to Adam. In other words, it is like the body. It is an external object of the relative realm. However, because there is no global foundation, it cannot work through this external object of the relative realm.

There are two reasons for this.

In the end, a family, a nation, and a country united with God... Even if God enters the family as He pleases, there must be no opposition from Satan, and He must be able to enter and exit the nation at any time without opposition from Satan.

What about our Unification Church? Does God act freely with the Unification Church? Look at this time. Does the teacher act freely with this time? "No." So it is Satan, Satan. You must understand that, in terms of principles, God's restoration providence has been difficult. Therefore, you must understand that until now, God has suffered and sacrificed countless prophets and sages.

There are many Americans here. If you thought, "Ah, the world or anything, as long as America is good," where do you stand? You are standing in a national position, not a cosmic position. Can God freely manage the world with this? No. The remaining fields are your conditions for judgment. Therefore, even if it means sacrificing the nation, we must save heaven and earth. To save heaven and earth means to seek God's will. If we do not do this, everything will disappear. Everything will perish. No matter what, everything will perish.

That is why in our Unification Church, centered on the restoration of the cosmos, individuals serve the family, the family serves the tribe, the tribe serves the nation... You must clearly understand this principle.

Have a clear purpose.

If there are Unification Church members around the world... Will the Unification Church members around the world gather together to say, "Let's live well"? "Yes." Without saving the world? Even if we gather like this, we must save the world to live well; we cannot live well before saving the world. Until then, we must sacrifice. No matter how much you try to live well, it is God who sacrifices you for the sake of the world.

The Unification Church cannot rest before saving the world. There is no other way. There is no other way. Now, is there another way? "No." Some people say, "Oh, I have been in the Unification Church for ten years, and I have suffered until now, and now you want me to go again; I cannot go." But is there a principle that says, "You have suffered for ten years, so rest"? "No." If you cannot go, it must be, "Go again, you brat! What are you doing, go!" You must push and shove to drive them out. That is the way for your own survival. The way for your own survival is that path.

You would not want it to be that way, right? "No." If that happens, your children, descendants, and even the nation will be affected. What if the teacher disappears too? It cannot be done for thousands or tens of thousands of years.

Do you know the path you are taking? Do you know the path of indemnity and restoration? "Yes." Then will you not worry? Do you know the teacher's path? "Yes." You must know the path the teacher is taking. You must understand why we are taking this path, why the teacher is doing this work, and why the teacher is gathering people from around the world and making them suffer in America. Do you understand?

What was the first thing I mentioned earlier? Purpose. Now you know the purpose. The purpose must be clear. Do you understand? "Yes." Is there one path or two? "One." It is one path forever and ever. It is one path. If you cannot align with this and go, you will become a wandering spirit in the spirit world, and you will have to align with it on this earth for eternity.

Centered on the teacher, there are individuals and families, and now the family has been established. The tribe has also been established. Next, we are working to establish the national realm and unite it with the world realm. That is why the teacher has left Korea. I have left, right? "Yes." And the children have been brought here based on this principle for three years. Thus, we have now only laid the spiritual foundation. However, if America becomes one externally, the world will completely become one.

So does our Unification Church have the content to do that? Yes, it has more than enough. So, how far have we come? (Pointing to what he wrote) We have come this far. Therefore, gathering people from all over the world, centered on all the nations, we are currently working on how to create a representative form and how to influence the world; this is the three-year course. You must understand this. We must create this to serve the world... Once the world becomes one, then the cosmos will naturally become one.

So what is the biggest problem in this world? It is not the lack of people. It is not the lack of power. The problem is the lack of purpose and values. The question is, what kind of world do we want to go to? The problem is the value system, the value system. Isn't that right? "Yes."

Then where is America going? We have reached a stage where democracy will not work. Where is communism going? Communism is the same. In the journey of humanity, if God exists, it cannot be based solely on the claims of ideologies established by humans. It must be the conclusion that there must be claims of ideologies established jointly by God and humanity. That is the principle of nature.

Because God is unchanging, the ideologies claimed in the past, those claimed now, and those that will be claimed thousands or tens of thousands of years later are the same. It is God's ideology to act freely centered on individuals, centered on families, and centered on the world.

So where must God and humanity meet? Ultimately, this is the end, the end. It is a global end. Do you understand? "Yes." Because it is a global end, there are also individual ends, family ends, tribal ends, national ends, and so on.

So, do you have an individual end? This is the intersection point where true people and evil people completely transition. So, have you completely met your individual end? Have you completed it? "Yes." Really? Where are you now? Are you really in a good position? "No." Then how can you say "yes"? Can you answer like that? Can you or can't you? If you have not met your individual end, can you go to the family? Has the tribe completely become good people? Have you completely completed it without receiving Satan's accusations? It is not done. That is why you must absolutely love the central being. Do you understand what that means?

This has not been completely settled yet. Even the nation has not been settled. All of this is still being carried along. Therefore, at some point, you must completely settle it. So you must leap from here to there, leap. (While writing on the board) If you absolutely unite with the path the teacher is taking, you can cross over. There is no other way. Is there another way? That is why Jesus said, "Be absolutely obedient before God. Be prepared to give your life." Do you understand? "Yes." Now you have clearly understood the purpose.

There is only one direction to go for the purpose.

Next, regarding direction... Is there one direction or two? "One." You have understood that. Ah, I must go for the family, I must go for the tribe, and therefore I must sacrifice for the family, sacrifice for the tribe, sacrifice for the nation, and sacrifice for the world. That is why religion calls for sacrifice.

What should blessed families do? They should unite and cooperate with each other for the sake of the nation and the world, and they should be able to encourage each other collectively. Such families are ideal families. Such a lifestyle is an ideal family life. Is that an ideal? Is that an ideal? "Yes." That is a forced answer. However, it cannot be done. You must go.

If you say, "I will go alone. I will only take care of my family," can that work? "No." Even if you go to heaven, you will be told, "Hey, you brat! Go back and bring them!" Because Jesus could not have a family, He must establish a family and lead the tribe and nation, but because He could not, He could not go to heaven and must come back.

If you cannot go, you will have to come back again. Would you like to come back again, or would you prefer not to? "I would prefer not to come back." You will not be able to come back in the future. The time to come back has passed. There is a principle that allows you to come back before the parents come out, but after surpassing the standard of completion, it cannot be allowed. If Adam and Eve had not fallen and had completed, could there have been a providence of salvation? "No." Therefore, after surpassing the standard of completion, there is no such time.

Now, you have understood that there is such a tremendous purpose in this universe, and that there is only one direction, that this direction is the only one. So do you want to get married or not? "I want to." What do you want to do after getting married?
Are you trying to? "I am trying to sacrifice." It is not about sacrificing alone, but both must come together to sacrifice. 
If Jesus had a bride when He was crucified and she also went to the cross, what do you think would have happened? There would be no need for ascension. If a family had been established on earth, there would be no need for ascension. If a couple had been formed on earth, there would be no need for the Holy Spirit to come; everything could be done on earth. There is no need to wait. It does not take such a long time. Because we have established the standard of spiritual parents on earth, we can freely act within that spiritual standard, allowing us to quickly occupy the world of Satan. And Christianity does not need to shed much blood. 
So, does that mean our Unification Church is just about making money and living well? "No." How about it? Even if we make money and evangelize, why do we need to do more? It is to save the world. So what kind of teacher am I? Even if you bring me money, I won’t say thank you; I will tell you to earn more. Even if you evangelize, I won’t say, "Hey, you worked hard," but rather, "Do more." Why is that? Is it because of me? "No." It is because of us, because of you and your descendants. 
Let’s run towards our goal at maximum speed. 
Next is speed. How fast do we want to go? Would you prefer it to take a year or a month? "A month." It will take effort, but will you stand still and walk quickly? Would you rather sleep for eight hours or two hours? Which one will you choose? "Two hours..." (laughter) Try it. (laughter) Do you want to run like this or walk like this? "Quickly." When you look, do you want to see like this or like this? How much speed you put in is the issue. I wish it could be done quickly... Wouldn't it be nice if we could quickly save all of America and freely control the world? "Yes." 
It took America 200 years. It took a full 200 years to build it. Countless American citizens came together and sacrificed... This means that with our small number, we need to put in dozens or hundreds of times more effort. 
So what will I do? Behind me, there is the spirit world. I mobilize the spirit world to do this. Do you think the spirit world is in the billions? (laughter) The spirit world can cooperate... Therefore, you must have absolute faith, believing that America is at my feet, that this world is at my feet. (As he steps on the ground, laughter follows.) 
Do you have that mindset? "Yes." Then God will cooperate with you. If you have that mindset, you will be the most formidable force in the world. Now, look. If you unite around the purpose, if all these people unite... Has there ever been a group in history that united around such a purpose? However, even if you die now, the principle that I have spoken will remain before humanity. 
It is similar to having already attacked the world of Satan with atomic bombs. It is like bombing. Why? Because all people have died. In the midst of that, we are restoring. If we move like this, more people will come to fear us. And when we say "Wow!" we will achieve victory. You are that group, but you do not realize that you are that group. You do not know that right now. 
Did we think we were such a formidable group? Did we think the world of Satan feared us the most? Feel that way. The world of Satan thinks that when we say "Wow!" it will collapse. Isn’t that a good feeling? "Yes." Even if we suffer, we should suffer and say, "That’s cool!" Even if we suffer, we should try again. 
The more we suffer, the more opportunities for leap will arise. It will be a leap forward. We will fly over. Such things will happen. Therefore, we are truly in a wonderful era... Now, let’s speed up and shorten the distance! Shall we shorten it or extend it? "Shorten it." What kind of full speed are we talking about? "Rocket." Without eating a meal? A rocket is like that. Can you run like a rocket without eating a meal? (laughter) We need to run faster than a rocket! (laughter) We are a rocket that runs without fuel. God cooperates... 
Because I have this purpose, I come to America to work; thinking about the hardships I endured in Korea until now is tiresome. I can never forget it, even if I die. Yet, I am suffering again in America. Look. I am working in America, and the FBI and CIA are watching Mr. Moon with glasses, wondering what he is doing. 
Did I come here to make a lot of money? Did I come to live comfortably? I have not had a moment to rest during this two-week speaking tour. Even today, when I promised to come here yesterday, I didn’t realize the day had come faster, and I went to bed late last night. I am only sleeping an average of two to three hours. Even that is not proper sleep. And still, I am fine. 
The idea of sleeping for eight hours is a dream for me. No way. I can manage with just two hours of sleep. At three o'clock, I wake up even while dozing off. I am trained like that. 
I hope you all create such love. Would you like me to help you do that? "Yes!" Then what will you do? First, use that time for God, and second, use that time for humanity. That is the only purpose. God and humanity—there are only these two purposes. 
Because God has received help from me and humanity has received help from me, I am in debt. Therefore, I must repay it. Even if I go to the spirit world, God will repay me, and humanity will repay me... That is the principle of nature. It will repay as it should. 
You wanted speed. Right? "Yes." Do you know football? When playing football, do you prefer to kick gently or to kick hard? This is about trying to make two meet. It’s exhilarating. So, would you prefer to be kicked hard or gently? "Hard." Don’t complain like a ball. (laughter) Does the ball complain? If you kick high, it flies high. If you kick gently... It absolutely obeys. It does not disobey. 
But when humans kick, they all react like this. (gestures) That’s not it. When you try to kick, you retreat. You should run to kick, but instead, you try to retreat, you little rascal! (laughter) Isn’t that right? Complaining and all. There are many people like that. Let’s not do that this year. Let’s see who here will not do that. Wonderful! Then among the people here, it means there will not be a single person falling behind this year. Huh? (laughter) 
Even if the Taesan mountain range is in the way, do not avoid it. 
Next is the environment. So, would you prefer a good environment or a bad one? "A good one." (laughter) Are we going to go to flat land or fill in the pits? "Fill in the pits." We are not going to flat land; we are going to fill in the pits as we go. The question is how to deal with the environment. If there is flat land on the way, there will be valleys, and if there are valleys, there will be high places. Sometimes, rocks block the way, and thorns block the way. Sometimes, legs break. Sometimes, faces get scratched. Sometimes, we even die. 
Then when I am about to die, will I say, "God, I am trying to fulfill the restoration providence, so why are you letting me die? Please save me!"? "No." Will I say, "Do not let me die, but let the person I hate the most die"? "No." No matter how much the environment changes, we go. Whether it’s night or day, we go. There must be both day and night for it to be 24 hours. If there is a bright time, there is also a dark time. Knowing that, even if the Taesan mountain range blocks your path, do not try to avoid it; you must face it normally. 
Now, if you encounter such an environment and get hurt, can you say, "Why did I get hurt? I did it because the teacher told me to, so it’s the teacher’s fault"? "No." It is not because of the teacher. It is because of the fall. Because of the fall, humanity has a shared responsibility, and that is why we are playing this game. 
Many people who believe in the Unification Church, when they find themselves in trouble, blame the Unification Church teacher and say all sorts of things. Such people receive double punishment. The teacher is suffering more than they are, and the teacher is doing harder work than they are... 
Therefore, even while dying, one must say, "Teacher, I am sorry." That is how one can find a way. One must say, "God, I am sorry." The teacher also says, "God, I am sorry." We must go like this, but... Knowing the path we must take, if one can say, "If I can die for God, if I can die for the teacher, if I can die for humanity, then if I, who am lacking, can do that, it would be an honor," that is the path of a rightful death. 
It is a remarkable fact that Jesus died for God, for humanity, and for enemies. Therefore, those who come from abroad find life in America difficult, but even if America is unfamiliar, they must strive to achieve results beyond their capabilities. 
These are the four principles. No matter who tries to cancel this purpose from me, even if I die a thousand or ten thousand times, this purpose that comes from a valid theoretical result cannot be taken away from me, and I cannot deny it. After that, there is only this one direction; to achieve this quickly, I must die, and there is no other way to die but the cross. This is how we must think. From this perspective, we can understand that Jesus carried the cross and sacrificed Himself because it was a path He had to take. 
You must shout "Long live the restoration of the universe!" as you die, restoration of the universe. That purpose is God's purpose. That direction is the direction God is going. All the effort God has put in until now is for that purpose. Therefore, we must realize that God has been paving the way of the cross until now, and we are also paving that environment from the same standpoint. 
On that path, on the way toward that purpose, no matter how sad and lonely I may be, even if the world does not recognize it, God knows. By doing so, God secretly entrusts everything to me. It is not that He gives it to me after I go to the spirit world; He gives everything to me on this path. Therefore, I must see that purpose more clearly than God, I must try to go more directly than God, I must try to go faster than God, and I must do more difficult things than God... Try to do it this way. When that happens, God can exercise unimaginable creative power, miracles, and wonders. 
Ultimately, if you become those who can comfortably accompany God, the path you take will become a remarkable path where you can inherit everything from God. It is not about asking God, "What will you give me?" and receiving it; even if we do not want it, God gives it to us. That is the position of reward. 
At that time, how great will God’s love be! At that time, how great will my gratitude be! Then God will be happy to give, and I will be grateful to receive, and I will be able to receive and give to the world. 
Now, will you go to heaven and say, "God, give me!" and receive it, or will you receive it here and take it with you? "Here." If you do such things, God will already give you everything without you knowing it. And to be such sons and daughters, God will proudly say to all creation, "Hey, you all, follow our sons and daughters. This child has done this and that." You must understand that you will be determined as beloved sons and daughters. 
Consider how serious it is to save the world and the heavens and the earth when your own sons and daughters are in a position to die. When you think of the world and your sons and daughters, the world is bigger... Therefore, understand God’s heart that He would sacrifice Jesus to save the world, and realize how anxious and painful the path we must take is, and I hope you resolve that you cannot avoid it. 
This path is the path we must take, and by doing so, we meet with God as individuals, meet in families, meet in tribes, meet in nations, meet in the world, meet in the universe, and become the kind of person who can be welcomed anywhere in the east, west, north, and south. This is the highest path our lives should take. The world becomes my stage, and the heavens and the earth become my stage. Isn’t that the highest path we desire in life? That is the highest path we must take as human beings. 
Will there be borders there? "No." Will there be issues of black and white? "No." Will there be distinctions between Eastern and Western people? "No." There are none. That is the place we must go. It is the highest path we must take as fallen humans. You must clearly understand this, and especially in 1974, as Unification Church members from all over the world come to America to work, I hope you will align with the teacher. And I hope you will head straight toward the path that heaven desires, shortening all the difficulties and creating flat land for a vigorous march, advancing toward the happy place we hope for. I briefly spoke about this. 
A year generally has 52 weeks, and today is the first Sabbath of this year, so we must spend the remaining time vigorously. 
Now, let’s advance vigorously. Have you made that resolution? "Yes!" 
<Prayer> Beloved Father, no matter how vast the heavens and the earth may be, I cannot help but think that the one point, the core, the center you desire is this place where the members of the Unification Church gather today.

We understood that this is a holy intention to expand that into one individual, one family, one tribe, one nation, one world, and to unite the entire universe, connecting the garden of heart centered on you.

We earnestly ask that all matters that come and go align with Your will. We thank You for allowing us this time today, and we pray all these words in the name of True Parents. Amen.

The path God takes and the path humans take

I know that it is cramped here, and I understand that you might find it boring. Over there, it may be narrow, but I hope you won't cry or complain about it.

Now, let’s talk a bit.

Thanks to the sincere prayers of many family members in our homeland, I have returned in good health. Even before landing at Gimpo Airport, I felt a different sadness as I looked down at the Korean land from the airplane.

This is because I felt a significant sense of guilt returning before you all. Since I took all the children to America, the family members back home must have felt quite lonely, and the Cheongpadong church must have felt quite empty.

When the whole family had children, even when praying, they focused their prayers on Korea rather than America, but now we are in a position where we must pray primarily for America.

It is natural for a Korean who does not know the situation in America to pray sincerely for this foreign land, and of course, it is because the teacher is there and his family is there, but I think they must have felt a deep sense of regret and loneliness, and I felt sorry for that.

February 8, 1974 (Friday), Central Training Center (Sutaek-ri).

In that sense, I would like to express my sincere apologies to you all at this time. However, you must understand that the position I have taken is not due to personal circumstances of the teacher.

The process of entering the United States, which had to go through many twists and turns

Originally, when I left for the United States in 1972, I did not inform the family members, but I felt a special command from God and a sense of responsibility to fulfill a historical mission regarding America for three years.

I understood that the question of how to set the direction for the American people toward a new Christianity and a new faith was God's will, so I went alone to that vast country. However, I could not help but think that influencing an entire nation and presenting a certain direction was difficult and impossible by human power.

Nevertheless, believing in God and without telling anyone here in Korea, I quietly resolved, "When I go to America, I will do this and that."

The journey was so difficult that problems arose from the moment I left Gimpo Airport. I might not have been able to leave, but due to special circumstances, I left and stopped in Japan, where more problems arose. However, to enter America, I needed a visa, which did not come out. Knowing that there was a divine will that I must enter, I had to find a way to enter America by any means necessary. But it was not easy, so I tried to enter Canada to open that path. I brought our Unification Church members in Canada to confront the embassy.

Thus, I caused a problem with the U.S. State Department to find out what the internal report on Mr. Moon was and what the State Department was holding that prevented my entry.

The report from the State Department stated that Mr. Moon could not enter because he had cooperated with the communists since 1967.

When I saw this fact, it was reported that someone named Moon from the Unification Church had cooperated with the communists. So they used that as a condition to attack me. I contacted U.S. agents by phone and had them attack the U.S. embassy in Canada from all sides.

They contacted their headquarters, and it became quite a big issue. It even reached the Korean embassy.

When it was revealed that their report was not true, they had no choice but to issue me a visa to enter the United States. If it had been extended for just a few days, I would not have been able to enter.

Seeing that, I felt that the evil forces, or the invisible satanic forces—those who are new here may not know this—were opposing the path to establish God's will in every possible way.

So, when I was trying to go from Canada to Washington, there were no flights available. At that time, our Little Angels were scheduled to perform at the Kennedy Center on December 18, 1971. I had to arrive somehow, but on that very day, there were no flights, so I had no choice but to take a twin-engine plane and fly very low through the mountain valleys, arriving after six hours. Thus, I was able to enter America.

Activities in America to present the historical direction for the future

At that time, the American members thought that since the teacher was not familiar with the American situation, even if he came to America, they should continue to do what they had been doing and could not even dream of holding a great revival or causing major issues. The missionaries in America also believed they should proceed according to the American situation.

So I instructed them, "I will do things my way, and you must follow my instructions. I am in a position where I must move according to what I decide, so do not hesitate and move according to the direction I present."

However, after giving such instructions, I noticed that because they were well aware of their country's situation, my words did not resonate in their minds, and they hesitated in their actions.

So I went directly to New York, contracted with Lincoln Center, and started a series of lectures in seven major cities in America from February 6, 1972. That was quite an adventurous move.

After that, I went through England and Germany, returned home, and in November 1972, I crossed back over to take on the responsibility of holding a second-year revival in 1973. So in 1973, I selected 21 cities and held revivals in each, which ended on January 28, 1974. Since there was only a two-week period after that, I used that time to go through England and Japan to come to Korea.

Now, starting from February 15, I must begin the 1974 grand tour again. So I have already set 40 cities to visit. Therefore, I cannot stay here for a long time.

The reason I started such work is not for any personal desire or for the revival of the Unification Church. It is because there was a significant purpose to present a new faith direction that must be established in the beloved America of God, which has led to a nationwide issue.

Now, if we mention "Reverend Moon" to the American people, it seems that he is quite well-known. Issues involving the media and other unexpected problems have arisen, creating a nationwide concern. Moreover, the Watergate scandal truly created a significant historical storm.

Thanks to the members of the Unification Church both domestically and abroad who followed the teacher's instructions and coordinated well, the American media and all high-ranking officials have begun to apologize for underestimating our movements, both over the phone and in print.

Seeing this, I realized that our movements thus far have had a considerable impact on them. This will not end here; in the future, you in Korea...

The reason I went to America was not for the development of our Unification Church. It was not to develop the Unification Church as a responsible leader to boast about it. It was solely to carry the great mission of how to present the historical direction that the world must take in the future.

Therefore, I could not speak about such matters to anyone. I have silently fought with this in my heart without saying anything. However, God has moved the environment in ways that humans cannot imagine, and now the global issue is at hand, making me realize once again that God raises history in ways that humans cannot understand.

To guide Asia on its path, I have been pioneering behind the scenes for seven years.

Now, we must think that our Unification Church must change from the past position of the Unification Church. When you pray, of course... The reason the teacher's family is all in America is for the future of Korea and, further, for Asia. During this trip, I reached a compromise with Kishi.

When considering this crucial issue, which is how to present a new direction to the Asian empires and how to overcome and transition into a new world, I believe we are now in a position where we must follow that direction from a new perspective.

The prayers you offered for Korea, the prayers you offered for the teacher who guided you, have surely not changed in sincerity toward God, but you must not feel regret that the direction has changed.

If you observe the situation in Asia, after meeting with someone significant in Japan, I can tell you that Japan will find itself in a very difficult position in the future. Centered around Karafuto, there are 240,000 Soviet soldiers, over 70 ships, and about 120 submarines stationed there. If they mobilize all of that, they already have the naval power capable of sweeping Japan away in an instant. Today, I see news reports that Soviet aircraft have invaded Japanese airspace.

And as we look at the spring, we see that the communists are preparing for a major strike, indicating that the fate of the nation is in a precarious situation.

If Japan is swept away by the Soviets, what will happen? And what about Korea? Korea will simply fall as it is.

Therefore, since 1965, I have been warning through Kishi that "Japan must go this way," and even after the Tanaka government came into power, I informed Kishi and Fukuda of this, which the Korean people do not know.

Perhaps those here see me, Teacher Moon, as someone who is being criticized in Cheongpadong, but I have spent seven years behind the scenes, shedding tears and facing rejection, to pave the way for Asia to follow the path that God desires.

Looking at the Unification Church in Japan, it is not that impressive. However, the fact that someone like Kishi can drive his car and visit there is due to the fact that what I have been saying has become a reality, and the situation in Asia has evolved as I described.

When we look at this reality, the question is who will first lure Japan between China and the Soviet Union. If they can bring Japan under their control, they will be able to dominate the Asian empires, which is why the Soviets cannot avoid taking risks here. Therefore, I warned the high-ranking officials in Japan, "You must never betray America. No matter what happens, always rely on America." However, the failure of the current diplomatic policy of the Tanaka government proves this.

We must be able to love the people of the world as we love the Korean people.

When we look at all of this, our Unification Church was not simply named after a good noun. Looking at Christianity until now, it has been divided into hundreds of denominations, and that Christianity has become self-centered.
The concept of a God-centered absolute monarchy, with a unique church authority, is nearly impossible to unify within Christianity. While we are well aware of this historical fact, it becomes possible when God intervenes. This is what we have believed and come to understand.

For this reason, you must not let your hearts become slack just because there is no teacher or family in the future. We must engage in decisive, earnest prayers with God. If the living God exists and loves our Korean people, we must fight in prayer over the issue of how to resolve the division of our nation.

If God is with us today, there is nothing we cannot accomplish. During the year and seven months of the teacher's activities in America, we have witnessed results beyond human imagination, confirming that nothing is impossible when God is involved.

From this perspective, you must renew your resolve and determination, moving to a level where you can love the people of the world as you love the Korean people. You must recognize that this is the time to transition.

When I left Korea for America, the greatest pain I felt was whether I could treat foreigners with the same pure emotional flow as I do with you. In an environment where daily emotions do not connect and language does not flow freely, in a land like America where various races intermingle, can we connect with them with the same heart as we did with you? The issue is how to cultivate a heart that can love these Americans even more than those who loved you.

From God's perspective, considering His will, between the Korean people and the American people, while Korea may have a central responsibility in the providential will, when viewed from a global historical responsibility, Korea can only fulfill a partial responsibility but cannot take on a global historical one.

From this viewpoint, it seems that God's love and belief in the world is greater than His love and belief in Korea. Therefore, just as God loves America more, if I do not have the standard to align my heart with God's love for America, then is it not futile to claim to fulfill God's will? I have lived with this understanding until now.

One thing I have learned is that when the purpose is the same, when the perspective on the purpose is the same, and when the paths we take in life are the same, people can unite. People are all the same. Whether they are Easterners or Westerners, when an Easterner cries, a Westerner also cries; when an Easterner laughs, a Westerner laughs too; when an Easterner feels pain, a Westerner feels pain as well.

Therefore, the issue is this: for those who can feel shared emotions of joy, anger, sorrow, and pleasure centered around the heart, it is possible to transcend nations and the world, to feel together, to act together, and to unite as one.

Having lived from this perspective, I have found that Americans and foreigners can be more pure and honest than Koreans. I have guided many people and have led many Korean youths, but I felt that they are quite easygoing, though it is unfortunate. Koreans tend to be swayed this way and that. Even when they clearly recognize the truth, they may still resist it, questioning, "What truth is that?"

However, Westerners are not like that. In this regard, they are quite pure. I feel that this is because they stand on a moral foundation due to Christian thought.

Moreover, after working in America, I found that unlike Koreans, when something is reported in the newspapers, it is done with purity. If there are any journalists present here, they do not view things through colored glasses. They see things as they are.

Thus, when we speak, if I say something is right and someone else says it is right, it is accepted as right; if I say something is right and someone else says it is wrong, we are encouraged to discuss it face to face. They do not simply react to one side of the argument.

Today, our Unification Church is facing all sorts of criticism in Korea. Those who come here for the first time may think, "Oh, that person is the so-called Reverend Moon of the Unification Church. Oh my! He is the one who spread those terrible rumors in the past." Yes, I am that person. (Laughter) You might have thought I was just a fool dancing naked, but far from it! If we speak with sincerity, I have cultivated a higher level of intellect than you, and if you seek justice, I have sacrificed my life more than you. I am a man who has poured all my wealth into this cause, like a gambler who risks everything. What else would I do if I were not engaged in this work?

Therefore, if you want to dance along with the rhythm, go ahead. I do not make excuses. Because I do not make excuses, people think I am a fool.

Our Unification Church members have endured a lot of sorrow until now. If it is unfair, we have faced unfairness. When I think about this, I feel a deep sense of frustration as a citizen of the Republic of Korea, as a member of the Korean people, and as a patriot who loves this nation.

However, because there is God's providence in this land of Korea, and because I love this providence, I have come to understand that I cannot help but love it. I have gritted my teeth and endured hardships in silence to shape the destiny of this country. No one among you in the Unification Church knows this. You do not know what I am doing. I do not speak about it now.

Even when dealing with Chiang Kai-shek, I sent people for talks up to three or four times, and even he did not know. I told him, "Your country will perish if you do not do this." This led to all the guards around him hiding, and those who went for talks were captured, leading to various incidents, all for the sake of Asia... all for Korea.

Our Unification Church members must understand this. The person known as the teacher has not lived like a drifter in a corner of Cheongpa-dong. Therefore, in preparation for future operations in America, I have been working hard and preparing to take the lead.

Such matters should be handled with the power of the state, but since the state does not know and does not act, someone must take on this responsibility, no matter how severe the trials may be...

Look! Just this time, even with the Watergate declaration, the Washington Post scoffed. "What? Reverend Moon from Korea? What is this?" The New York Times thought it was only in the Washington Post and the New York Times. But it was published in newspapers across all 50 states.

To do this requires a lot of money. It is not that I do not care about money. I know that our Unification Church members are starving in Korea. I know they cannot even eat barley rice. I understand that what we have is more precious than blood and more valuable than life.

However, for the sake of God's will, I resolved to give my all, even if it meant becoming a pillar of salt. While there were not many members across the nation, when I first went to America in 1972, there were only 300 members. In a year and a half, I was able to grow that number to 2,300. Now, if all those sent abroad are included, we have created a base where 3,000 can operate and demonstrate in Washington... This is why they are now afraid. The Unification Church members across all 50 states can concentrate in one place within 48 hours.

With this, members of Congress, those who make a fuss, and the entire media are all intertwined... even poor Nixon... I have heard the term "pro-Nixon" until now, but I am not pro-Nixon. Have I ever met Nixon? Did I write him a letter? Others think that Nixon gave me money to fund this work, but that is not true. History will testify that I did this work by selling my blood.

Therefore, now I can meet Nixon in Washington as many times as I want. After finishing revival meetings in 15 cities, I arrived in Washington on the 28th, and during the next three days, his aides rushed to see me. Now, they cannot ignore Mr. Moon.

Now, the future operations must be developed with your prayers. Do you understand? "Yes." I will stop here for today. (Laughter)

From now on, President Park of Korea should consult with Reverend Moon of the Unification Church... to take Korea beyond Asia and into the world, becoming a leader of global thought. Even if the country is divided, this nation—though small in appearance, and seen as poor by Westerners—can become a nation that no other can compete with if the people of the Republic of Korea unite ideologically.

When I went to Washington and investigated the Korean community, I found many doctors. However, they have become mere "rice bugs," not knowing where their homeland is, not knowing where the Republic of Korea is... But when you look closely, they are quite intelligent. There are over 300 political science doctors, right? In any case, they have studied well. Wouldn't it be great if these people could unite and educate Asians?

Now, I will lay the foundation from that perspective. How will I do that? I cannot explain how, but I will do it. If I say I will do it, I will do it. While the Korean community may oppose the Unification Church... I am not doing this because I am inferior to established church pastors. I am not doing this out of envy for anyone in Korea.

Now! Knowing this, the time has passed when the teacher fought alongside you, sweating for Korea. Now...

The Unification Church members are strong in theoretical punches.

The world is currently in turmoil. America is also in chaos. The churches are all on the brink of collapse. And looking at the entire world, I know that communists are dreaming of world domination in the coming years. Who will stop this? No one can, so it must be God. We must believe in God and plant a flag, even if we are a minority. We must pave the way for this... because someone must do this work.

From this perspective, even if the teacher has left Korea to go abroad, do not feel resentful... Instead, I will try to come back whenever I can. In fact, I have felt quite sorry compared to before. When I try to pray for Korea, there are many times when tears obscure my vision. So! Understand this...

Now, our persecuted Unification Church must unite. We must unite and embrace this nation, struggling alongside God, fulfilling our mission to become one.

Therefore, I hope that you, who love this country even more than the teacher, will become patriots who will endure any criticism and face any storm with a heart of absolute dedication and loyalty. Do you understand? "Yes."

Now, most of the people gathered here are young. The teacher is now over 50. I have faced many challenges this time as well, but where is there time for rest? While continuing to face challenges, I think, "How great it would have been if I had built this foundation in my 30s! If I had this foundation in my 30s in the Republic of Korea, today, Korea would not be like this." However, I do not despair. If you, who remain in the homeland, can fulfill the duty of loyalty and filial piety that the teacher wanted to carry out in his youth for God's will, it is not too late, and if you can take my place and achieve what I could not, that would be my wish.

Therefore, from this perspective, you must protect the country. If the Korean military had been spiritually armed with the ideology of the Unification Church, and if the people had been spiritually armed with this ideology, Asia would not be a problem.

When we demonstrated in Washington this time, over 2,000 gathered. Although it was a small number, even in the vast land of America, this is a significant issue. Moreover, our Unification Church members are strong in theoretical punches. They already have a worldview firmly established. They have the ability to critically assess their current position, and if they strike, even senators will retreat.

These are the people who can do this. In America, just imagine if we were ten times stronger. This is how we see it. Isn't that right?

So, when we ask whom God resembles, we can conclude that, of course, He resembles Himself, but that is vague. He resembles women and men. He resembles me.

Therefore, while God resembles humans, what is the difference? God has a heart and a body, but His heart and body never fight; they are in perfect unity. They are one. So, selling is equally difficult. Koreans know that ginseng tea is good, but they might say it is a bit expensive. They will say it is expensive, but once they realize how good ginseng is, the price will eventually rise...

Do not lose to the international mobile unit
That is why we have entered an international era. Do you understand? "Yes." Now, should the Korean people become laggards? Do not complain and believe that 'it can be sold. What the teacher says can be done.' Believe and pray to God. 'God, who can do anything! Today, I will load ginseng tea onto a truck and go out. There will be people in Seoul who will buy it. I may not be able to visit all 6.5 million people, but there will be some.' Believe that there will be people. There will be someone who will buy a truckload. 

The Japanese, you know, carry one case each and manage to sell a truckload in 70 days. The other day, I said, 'Hey! Stop being petty. Sell at least twelve cases.' We are promoting the movement to sell by the box... So now they are selling by the box, and they cannot even brag about it. 'How many boxes did you sell?' 'I sold three boxes today.' If they say that, they cannot hold their heads up. Selling three boxes only amounts to 36 bottles.

You guys, like, 'Oh, can't you do it?' (laughter) Think about it. Can you become a mobile unit leader by selling four bottles? That is frustrating, you guys. And all the mobile units are funded by the headquarters, right? In the future, the international mobile unit...
Well, the teacher's view is that we must unify everything. Otherwise, you do not have the qualifications to participate in the international mobile unit. So now, you must go back and ensure that each month, one person is evangelized, and then cultivate people who can help the church independently and send them out as mobile unit members. That is the international standard. It is the standard for Olympic athletes. Do you understand? "Yes." Besides supporting from a position of indebtedness, the teacher thinks we should select special members here and create a mobile unit of 70 that meets international standards, and we should do such things. Prepare for that. I will have to work hard in the U.S. until this year, but since I am busy going around... If we set this up, by the end of this year, Korea will be embarrassed by how much we have accomplished. So, do not lose, but run. Do you understand? "Yes."

I talked about ginseng tea, the responsibilities of leaders, the trainees, and the international mobile unit... What did I miss? I left my notebook behind... If I were to talk about all that, it would take all day... Even what I have said so far is enough for those who have not been able to do it; there is no need to mention it all. Just what I have said so far is enough to make your eyes droop and you sit there nodding off... (laughter)

Our movements and spiritual direction
So, when the teacher goes this time, I don't think I will be able to come for a year. During that time, what will the teacher do? I am really curious about that. Right now, I am paving the way, and when the day comes that this breaks out, on the day when the first, second, and third waves hit in succession, the world will be at my fingertips... This is what I am saying. I won't reveal what that is. Do you understand? "Yes."

I have a dream for the year, and I wonder what dream you have had for the year... When we meet again, I hope to be in front of you with my nose long and my head bowed, hoping you will leave such results. Do you want that? Are you confident? "Yes." How many of you are there? Are those foolish ones answering? Are you confident or not? "We are." First, I want you to answer with confidence. Are you confident or not? "We are." (laughter) Why are those who believe in God like this? God likes unexpected people, unexpected ones. Even stealing is done by unexpected people, while others are starving. If one person remains among all those who are starving and leaves behind seeds, that is not a sin. (laughter)

Now we have entered a stage where numbers are needed.
So, keep that in mind... It would be good if I could come once in April, but anyway, I need to lay the foundation to mobilize 4,000 people in New York over the next four months—April, May, June, July—and then prepare accommodations for those people, so this is a big deal. Although I have given directions, mobilizing 4,000 people is not easy. The day we mobilize 4,000 people will be something else... When we mobilized 400 people before, it stirred up all of New York, but when we mobilize 4,000 people... With 4,000 people, we will have one person sitting in every alley with a chair. They will be sitting there 24 hours a day. We will grab the people coming and going and ask, "Do you know the day (the day of the Madison Square Garden meeting)? Will you come that day or not?" and make them come... We can sit there and ensure that not a single pack can slip away.

Interestingly, in New York, you can't use any cars other than buses or taxis. When rush hour comes, there is a crowd, and even if you just stand still, you get pushed along. Therefore, if we grab the tail of that crowd and push them in one direction, we can automatically gather everyone in New York. I am trying to do evangelism like that in New York...

Madison Square Garden can hold 25,000 people, and if packed tightly, it can hold more than 40,000. If we pack them in, we will have to blow our feet and push them out... This costs ten thousand dollars. How much does it cost to rent for a day? It costs several tens of thousands of dollars.

Now that we are doing such things abroad, what do you, who are in this homeland, want to sell under what name? That won't do. So, we must run hard this year. Do you understand? "Yes." You have definitely made a promise, right? "Yes." You have definitely made a promise, right? "Yes." No more, just evangelize twelve people. Evangelize twelve people. Focus on that, focus on it. Even after eating, go find people... In Korea, there are always wives at home, right? Husbands have all gone to work, but the women are all at home, right? In America, there are no wives or husbands. If anything, there are just cats and dogs waiting for food, barking "woof woof." They carry keys around. It would be much easier to distribute houses like that in Korea.

Now that we have entered a stage where numbers are needed, I hope you will engage in serious activities centered around such standards so that you can meet the goals that God desires. Do you understand? "Yes."
