<Prayer> Beloved Father! I know that 1974 is a crucial time for the Unification Church, and we are at an undeniable point in time considering the internal and external circumstances. Father! Although the children scattered across the nation are doing their utmost to bear the heavenly mission, I know that they fall short of the standards and limits you desire. However, I sincerely hope and wish that you will love them and encourage them both internally and externally until the end, so that they can devote their sincerity and wisdom without shame before the historical mission.

Father! Please do not let this path we have returned to be in vain. These children have made new resolutions and commitments, so I earnestly hope that their journey will be blessed. Please protect and guide the path of the children who fight with their hearts set on Korea, America, and the Pacific in between, Father, I earnestly hope and wish.

The foreign members have expectations and hopes for Korea, so I sincerely hope that those in this homeland realize how much effort and loyalty they must pledge in 1974 to meet their expectations and hopes.

Father! May your permitted will flourish, allowing us to surpass the limits of 1974 and establish a victorious standard that can be boasted of to all nations.

Until we meet again, I ask that you personally guide, oversee, and protect us, and I pray all these things in the name of True Parents. Amen. *

Restoration's Summit
<Prayer> Beloved Father! Today is February 10, 1974, and on this second Sabbath morning of the month, we have gathered here with the children at the headquarters church.

We feel that we have a mission to keep all the years that have come and gone in accordance with your will and to fulfill the time of your wish, leading us to the historical path of restoration. Furthermore, considering that this place is one that children from all over the world admire, I earnestly hope and wish that your love, compassion, and blessings will be with the children gathered here in this humble place.

The children in East Garden are also thinking of this place and looking forward to the day we meet again, so please bless those children, Father.

May you unite Asia and the West, making them the barriers of victory in your will, so that you can resolve all the grievances you have not been able to resolve until now and proclaim the liberation of all mankind on that day, allowing this nation to stand together with all people of the world.

Father! I earnestly hope and wish that the countless spirits in the spirit world and the many children on this earth, along with the descendants to come, can become one in your love, creating the point of providence on earth in this year of 1974, February 10 (Sunday), at the headquarters church (Cheongpa-dong 1-ga).

* This message is also published in <Words> No. 158 (issued on March 25, 1974).
In this year of 1974, we must establish the authority of decisive victory, and I earnestly hope and wish that all the days of this coming year will be gathered as your days of victory, Father. Please take charge of this entire time. I pray in the name of True Parents. Amen.

<Words> Those living on this earth should know that they must walk the path of restoration through the Principle.

The summit of restoration is the position of Adam and Eve before the fall.
When we speak of returning to the original position, that original position is, of course, the position of Adam and Eve, but the position of Adam and Eve itself refers to the position before the fall. Therefore, that position itself will be the highest position as individuals, and then it will become the highest position as families centered on that, or it will be the origin from which tribes, nations, and the world can reach the highest position. You must think about this. In other words, that position is where one can dwell with God. The life from birth to death must always have a content that is in harmony with the heavenly world.

Thus, as we live in such a position, everything we see, hear, think, and feel through our senses is not a place that connects solely through the 'I' alone. The act of seeing itself must be centered on God's love, with God and me and all creation... Because humans are the center of the universe, we must maintain that position as the center of the universe at all times from that place where we are one with God.

Therefore, a person in such a position can stand in a place that can represent heaven, a place that can represent the earth, a place that can represent the universe, or a place that can represent the historical humans of future generations, or a place that can represent families, and then a place that can represent nations and states. Isn't that the position of Adam and Eve before the fall?

When you think about this, you realize how enormous this issue is. What we standardize today as we walk the path of restoration is how we can acquire the position of the summit of restoration within our living sphere. When you think about this, you must always have this overall thought and pray and strive.

Jesus represents the entire historical summit.
What has God been seeking for over 6,000 years? He has established historical ancestors through Abel's era, Noah's era, Abraham's era, Moses' era, and the era of Jesus, and what has he been seeking until now? Of course, he has come to resolve the standard of the summit of restoration that all of history desires, but in terms of the external aspects, he has expanded the external aspects, and through the chosen people's foundation, he has expanded into familial forms, national forms, and state forms. However, that family has not been able to become a family that stands at the summit of restoration, and the nation has not been able to become a standard that stands at the summit of restoration.

If Jesus comes with relative conditions, then every individual of the entire nation of Israel must become completely one with Jesus. In other words, Jesus came as one who represents the entire historical summit because he came to take the place of the unfallen Adam. Therefore, the true individual who can become one with Jesus, who stands as the center of restoration, is always a matter of concern.

Thus, you must become a true individual who can become one. To become such an individual, you must take Jesus, the central being, and regard him as the subject of your entire life, beyond your heart, and become one with Jesus.
We must become beings that can completely unite with Jesus as objective entities. Thus, I must become a relative existence that can automatically go wherever Jesus goes, even if I do not wish to.

By centering around Jesus' family, I must personally uphold and unite with it just as I personally desire. This must then pass through a form of a tribe, where the tribe upholds the standard of being one with Jesus' family, and then the nation upholds the standard of the united tribe, thereby expanding these relative conditions.

When we think about these issues, we see that what started centered on the individual expands into family, tribe, and nation. The question arises: will this rise upward, become a straight line, or descend? This outcome is inevitably shaped here. While it may be possible to draw a straight line based on the standard of being able to unite with Jesus centered on person-to-person, can that line remain straight forever? Of course, individuals may draw that line, but when it comes to families, can families draw that line? It becomes even more difficult for families. If tribes exist, it is even harder than for families, making it easier to descend. If nations exist, it becomes even easier to descend.

When we think about these issues and consider God's providence of restoration, even if we unite centered on the family based on that foundation of being one with the individual, how can we expand the foundation to rise along this straight line or plane? This is undoubtedly a significant challenge for God.

What has God sought throughout the historical ages? It is to find one Messiah. It is to establish one Messiah. In other words, it is to find a central being who can stand in the position of an original human being without the traces of the fall. If that one person achieves victory, it will not just be a victory for that person alone, but it will become a central being that can determine a cosmic victory. However, even if that being establishes the standard of victory, the question remains: how can the relative foundation be unified? This is an exceedingly difficult problem.

In this perspective, how much should we hope to unite around the returning Lord and the concept of the Second Coming? While it is unchanging that I unite absolutely as an individual relative to the returning Lord, when we consider the issue of families uniting around that individual, a difficult problem arises. We must recognize that a challenging problem emerges. Furthermore, even if families unite, is it not more difficult for families and tribes to unite? Is it not even more difficult for nations to unite? Is it not even more difficult for the world to unite?

When we think about these issues, how to establish the standard of the normal line of restoration, centered on the individual and family, becomes an important standard that those who welcome the returning Lord must follow.

Now, if the standards of uniting as individuals and families do not align and fall apart, what should we do? What will support this? It is undoubtedly difficult to rise. It is easy to descend, but how do we resolve this? This is a matter that the members of the Unification Church, especially the blessed families, must consider.

When there is one person and then two, opinions will emerge from those two people. If there are three people, there will be three opinions. If there are four people, there will be four opinions. The more people there are, the more difficult it becomes. When considering such problems, if the husband asserts himself and the wife asserts herself, it becomes clear that establishing such principles is an impossible path.

Thus, if we seek a solution here, what is it? It is the path of self-sacrifice. It is not the sacrifice of someone who says, "I am fine now. I have reached this point." Rather, it is the sacrifice of someone who feels inadequate and looks toward the hope they must pursue. Without this, it is exceedingly difficult to connect God's will along this straight line. We cannot help but think this way.

Therefore, when we look at the Unification Church from a principled perspective, the path to completion is to speak of a central position that can manage everything, guide everything, and take responsibility for everything. Can I truly fulfill the responsibility of achieving that standard of completion on the global stage of our time? That is exceedingly difficult.

If we consider this, how should our Unification Church sustain itself in the future? We must think that there is no other way but the path of sacrifice. Then, how can we prevent this descent through sacrifice? Even if we sacrifice, if we stand at the center, we may not achieve the relative conditions in reality, but there is a way we can achieve it in our hearts.

Why? Because God conducts the history of recreation centered on the center, and that history is a history of restoration. In other words, God recreates Adam centered on Himself and recreates Eve centered on that Adam. When we think about this process of recreation, if you have the materials to recreate, those materials cannot be the ones that assert themselves.

Even if there are elements, those elements remain as objective entities that move according to the owner's plan, whether to the left or right, forward or backward, depending on the movement of the subject. They cannot assert anything from their own position as objects. When we consider this, it becomes possible only if we stand in the position of a creature, as materials that must be created.

Therefore, anything that can assert itself cannot stand in the position of being completely created as an objective existence. If you place it here, it will inevitably assert itself, move, or change direction, making it impossible to achieve completion as a fully objective entity.

Thus, by sacrificing ourselves, by turning our entire being into nothing, we can always unite with the intention of the subject. We must think that there is a path where we can be recreated, grow again, and develop toward some purpose. Therefore, the conclusion that the Unification Church must also urge sacrifice on this path is established.

In making sacrifices, we must strive for complete sacrifice. If we achieve complete sacrifice, we will reach the standard of complete normality. If the subject surely emerges from the position of complete sacrifice, God will empower that subject to create relative beings before the existence of the object that has made complete sacrifice. If this history unfolds, it will surely remain as a being on the path of normality as an objective existence before that subject.

When we think this way, how vast is the mission the returning Lord must fulfill when He comes to this earth? How vast it is! When you think about the members of the Unification Church or the blessed families, how different is it before and after receiving the blessing? There is not much difference. When we cannot think, "I have stood in the absolute position that God can hope for," we realize that we must remain on the path of sacrifice in this restoration process.

To understand this, you should pray. You can clearly know whether this is true or not through prayer. When you enter a position of sacrifice and pray, if you encounter extreme difficulties from the opposite position of sacrifice, you must hold onto God in that extreme situation and pray with gratitude to overcome it. If you stand in a position of self-assertion there, it will end with just yourself.

Therefore, when you enter a difficult position, a sacrificial position, and go forth with the thought of going for the whole subject, you can recognize that a great power is at work. This is something you can experience when you stand in a position of prayer.

In the path of restoration, the purpose must be thorough and complete. Today, if you members of the Unification Church say, "I will absolutely not change centered on this will. The purpose has been established through the principle," if that is established, how do you maintain an unchanging self centered on that purpose 24 hours a day? This is an exceedingly significant issue.

A person who can stand before God... If God has a purpose, He does not think about that purpose in the morning and abandon it by lunchtime. He thinks about that purpose eternally. Because He is moving toward that purpose, whether resting or staying, He must always be advancing toward that purpose.

Thus, the posture of advancing always has a central line toward that purpose, and based on that central line, He will always align with it. When viewed from this line, even if one is moving toward the purpose, there are various directions one can go—upward, downward, or sideways.

Therefore, always moving toward the purpose, God Himself will also strive to move in that direction. Just as a compass always aligns itself toward the north, as one advances, it does not change.

When we look at it this way, we must first clearly understand that "the path of restoration must go like this: the individual must go like this, the family must go like this, the nation must go like this, and the world must go like this."

In this journey, while it is certainly necessary to seek and possess things, it is exceedingly difficult to break through this path by deciding and resolving things centered on myself while living there. Having everything is for the sake of walking this path, and living must also take on a lifestyle that aligns with this path. Without this, it is exceedingly difficult to align with this path. We cannot help but think about these issues.

Therefore, the more we think about the normality of restoration, the more we realize it is difficult to reach that position with what we have in the world. Thus, in order to go forward, if there is a subject, I must become one who can always move toward that established purpose and thorough direction from the position of nothingness. That must be the first... I must be thorough and complete regarding the purpose.

You need to realize that you are representatives who encompass the satanic world. You must have that awareness. When you say, "I am currently on a personal path of restoration. I am going toward personal completion based on the standard of personal normality," that realization must be clear to you. 

The history of God over 6,000 years is about finding one Adam. When we think about how hard it is to find one man over 6,000 years, we cannot help but realize how challenging the history of restoration is.

In this regard, you must think about the era you are in and where you are going. For the sake of the individual, our Unification Church members are going through a three-year or seven-year course. But what kind of period is this? It is a period of indemnity. Without complete indemnity, God cannot support my consciousness. Without standing on the standard of complete indemnity, there can be no resurrection of Adam, no resurrection of men, and no resurrection of women.

When we consider what complete indemnity is, the being that must achieve complete indemnity is not just me alone today. Because I am connected to this satanic world, where there are families, nations, and the world, we must have the awareness that "I am a representative who encompasses the satanic world."

Why? Because the returning Lord is the one who will represent the entire world, and to stand in that position, I must be a man who can represent the world or a woman who can represent the world. We must think this way. The central being coming from heaven does not carry the content of all indemnity, but I, as a being, appear with the content of indemnity. There is a stark difference, a difference between heaven and earth. How to align this is an exceedingly difficult problem.

Therefore, you must recognize that you are not just a random molecule in the world. You must realize that you are standing at the center of restoring the world. Next, how do you recognize that you are not just one of the 3 billion people but a central being who represents all 3 billion?

Thus, the mission of my existence is... God needs individuals to find families. It is to find families. The need for families is to find tribes. The need for tribes is to find nations. The need for nations is to find the world.

In this way, starting from myself and going out to find everything, we must return to the position where we can finally relate to the heavenly subject. Do you understand? You must think about this. After finding everything and returning, you must be called upon based on the foundation of having received God's approval, representing the world.
as a representative. This is the way we must return to God. Even though we should be returning to God, we are not able to do so... What are we thinking now? We cannot float away from here and remain behind. If that happens, my existence will have no relation to world history. This is the reality we face.

Today, this world is like a single tree, a fallen tree. This is one household, one household. So how can we connect this? We, the members of the Unification Church, must discover the fact that when we say 'I,' it must be for the family, for the nation, for the world, for heaven and earth, and for the sake of such an 'I.' Therefore, we represent the world, the nation, and then the family.

If we look at it this way, it becomes like a tower in a circular shape. It is like a pyramid. While it may appear flat, in a circular view, it can be that kind of 'I'... Standing in such a representative position, we should originally be one with the central being of heaven. This is the path of principles we must follow.

Why did Jesus have to die on this earth? Why did Jesus have to sacrifice himself? Based on this national standard, if there were tribes, families, and representatives of families, and if they had all united with Jesus, then Jesus could have made this nation his stage for a worldwide start. However, abandoning the nation, the ethnicity, and the family, it became all about 'me,' just 'me'... This is not the normal course of restoration. You must understand this. Therefore, you must always think that you are destined to stand as a central being and return.

The way for fallen humanity to return to God

When we think about this normal course of restoration, there is no direct way for us fallen humans to go. We cannot go directly. Even if you go with our Unification Church leader, it is not just about following the leader. You must bear your own cross, which remains at all times.

Therefore, being a son or daughter of God means that one must overcome the satanic world. So what is the satanic world? It is the individual satanic world, the familial satanic world, the worldwide satanic world, and the satanic world of heaven and earth. What this means is that Jesus must have triumphed over the entire world and only after appearing as a victor in a central position could he ascend to heaven. Because the Israelite nation could not fulfill that mission, Jesus had to go out to take on that mission... Knowing that Jesus would fulfill the will of heaven, the nation of the enemy, Satan, would inevitably seek to kill him. This is the historical reality we must understand today.

Therefore, when you pray, it is not for yourself. The very act of praying for yourself goes against the principles. Living for yourself also violates the principles. Therefore, I was born for the whole, I live for the whole, and I must decide my center for the whole. This perspective is absolutely necessary.

To reach such a position, you cannot go by asserting yourself. You can only manage this by sacrificing yourself.

From a principled perspective, this connects with the principles of creation. It is the way that aligns with the principle of God’s complete investment. To sacrifice means to need an object, and in order to create an object, to find a perfect object, you must invest everything, one hundred percent... Only by investing the complete can the complete come forth.

Therefore, 'You shall love the Lord your God with all your heart, with all your soul, and with all your might,' has been the teaching until now. However, that heart, to love the Lord your God with all your heart, soul, and might, does not end there. With that love, you must love individuals, love families, love nations, and love the world. And then you return.

Because Jesus could not do such work, he could not lay that foundation, so he must come again. When he returns, Christianity will have a worldwide foundation. Within that worldwide Christianity, there must be national Christianity, familial Christianity, and individual Christianity, forming a global shape of Christianity. Centered on this Christianity, when all representative standards are established and historically restored, only then can the way to return to God be opened. However, if we cannot become one, restoration will be repeated. You must understand this.

Only through sacrifice can we subdue the satanic world and return to the path of restoration.

Christianity has laid the foundation of restoration over its 2,000-year history, but because it has not aligned with God’s will today, our Unification Church is going through the third seven-year course centered on the 21 years of the restoration path. You must understand this.

As the leader goes through this process, whether centered on the individual, the family, the nation, or the world, what must be done? Everything must be managed, and we must return to the original position and stand in the center of the whole to find the way to become one with God. The path we take is the path of sacrifice. The question is how much we invest. You must understand that this is always a problem. Therefore, until we establish some heavenly foundation that can move the world with a nation, sacrifice is inevitable. Without it, without passing through sacrifice, we cannot find the way for fallen beings to return to the path of restoration.

Why do we sacrifice? It is to subdue the satanic world. After subduing, we must return. To do this, we must subdue on an individual level, on a familial level, and on a global historical level. You must understand this.

To enter the heavenly kingdom of restoration, we must establish a worldwide standard of restoration.

The reason I returned this time is... It is a significant issue that our Unification Church must determine some victory standards that can overcome on an individual, familial, tribal, national, and global level. This is why I came to Korea this time.

To solve this, what must be done? How can we create conditions that Christianity has not fulfilled? Or if the Republic of Korea has not fulfilled its responsibilities, how can we resolve this? There must be a way to resolve it. To do this, the person who resolves it must overcome that hill. The one who saves must go over that hill and enter a position where they can be saved, and there they must anchor or tie something. Only then can they return and perform the act of saving. Without overcoming this, there is no way to save.

**The Biblical Background of the Jewish Nation's Killing of Jesus**

Now, the question is how will the Lord come? We must understand this clearly. According to the Bible, it says that at the end, neither the Son of Man nor the angels know, but only the Father knows.

Therefore, there is a way to know how He will come by negotiating with God, and in addition, there is a way to find out through our human wisdom by inferring how the Messiah, the Lord, came in the past. You must understand that there are only these two paths.

Even if you enter the spiritual world and receive revelation from God, can you believe that? Even if Reverend Moon says that, it cannot be trusted.

Thus, it must be presented with solid evidence and truth-based support. Therefore, by knowing the Messiah who has come, we can infer the future. This is beyond question.

Today, the hope of Christianity for the Messiah to come is exactly the same as the position of the Jews 2,000 years ago who were waiting for the Messiah. Looking at Christianity today, it has been hoping for the Messiah to come for 2,000 years, but from the perspective of Judaism, heaven has sent many prophets for 4,000 years to sacrifice them, promising to send the Messiah.

God promised to send the Messiah for 4,000 years, so that nation has diligently believed that if He were to come, they would unite firmly to fulfill God's will.

Thus, God sent Jesus Christ, the Messiah, as promised before that nation. Furthermore, that nation was in a position to accept Him as promised. However, the nation that hoped for the Messiah did not accept Him but instead persecuted and killed Him. Isn't that a riddle?

To illustrate this event, today, Christians hope for the Lord to come, for the Messiah to come, but when the Messiah came, the highest leaders of Christianity, such as the Pope, cardinals, bishops, and various pastors, all mobilized to kill Him, resulting in the same outcome. Simply saying, "He came to die," does not suffice. It is theoretically incorrect.

Then, why would He come to die? After killing many prophets for 4,000 years and making the Israelite nation suffer so much... If He were sent to unprepared villains, how easily would they kill Him? It is impossible to answer with words.

Therefore, from now on, we must clearly understand why the Jewish nation, which had long awaited the Messiah, killed Him despite God sending Him. Do not take this too seriously just because you are hearing it for the first time. We must understand why they killed Him.

The reason they killed Him is, first, because the Old Testament foretold it. Why? As you know, the Old Testament corresponds to the New Testament's Revelation. In Malachi 4:5 and following, it is prophesied, "Before the great and dreadful day of the Lord comes, I will send you the prophet Elijah, and he will turn the hearts of the fathers to their children, and the hearts of the children to their fathers." We must understand this fact firmly.

Elijah is a person who ascended in a chariot of fire 900 years before Jesus came. Because God loves this people and has set the time to send Elijah, they expected Elijah to come down.

The Bible firmly states that Elijah would come, but Elijah did not come. What kind of book is the Bible? It has been the foundation of the Israelite national thought for 4,000 years, the center of Jewish faith, and a book that all life has poured into believing for 4,000 years. Can we discard this book after hearing the words of Jesus?

Would you believe that? What does that mean? It means that while they hoped for the Lord to come down from heaven on a cloud, someone came and said, "I am the Lord." Can Christianity believe that today?

Because of such an event, let us see whether Jesus was troubled or not through His words. Let us look at Matthew 17:10 and following. The disciples did not know the Scriptures well, did they? These ignorant ones believed in Jesus as the Savior and went out to preach, saying, "Oh, the Messiah has come, believe in the Messiah," but the priests who did not believe asked, "If your teacher is the Messiah, then according to the Scriptures, Malachi surely says that Elijah will be sent before the Messiah comes, but where is Elijah?" So, these ignorant ones, not knowing, asked Jesus and received an answer.

If Elijah had come, it would have been fine whether Jesus was serving or was deaf or lame. The problem is that Elijah did not come. Look at this. The Bible says, "When the disciples asked Him, 'Why then do the scribes say that Elijah must come first?' Jesus answered and said, 'Indeed, Elijah is coming first and will restore all things. But I say to you that Elijah has already come, and they did not know him but did to him whatever they wished... Then the disciples understood that He spoke to them of John the Baptist.'" (Matthew 17:10-13)

Is John the Baptist Elijah? Would you believe that?
312   A New Future for Christianity  
Elijah did not come, but they attach Elijah to John the Baptist. They say, "The reason you are associating John the Baptist with Elijah is to make him a fraud disguised as the Messiah."  
So they defined Jesus as a monster who ruined the chosen people of Israel established by God for 4,000 years and as the prince of Baal-zebub. Is that possible? "He must surely be the son of Satan. Who would believe someone who claims Elijah has come when Elijah has not come?" they say...  
The Jewish people who misinterpreted the Old Testament and killed the Messiah Jesus  
Until now, Judaism has been an enemy of Christianity. Here, we must understand what the Bible is.  
To create a person, family, or nation that can fulfill God's will in the world of Satan, they are in a position similar to that of an informant sent to an enemy nation. Therefore, when God gives them instructions, if they convey them as they are, everything will be completely ruined.  
That is why we must understand that the Bible is a record of God's instructions given in code. When the CIA sends an informant to the Soviet Union, do they write a letter saying, "Do it this way"? They send it in code.  
If the Lord had clearly taught how He would come until now, they would have killed the coming Lord. Because they did not know, because He taught them in code... At the end, He must create an environment where they cannot catch and kill Him, and there must be God's will to guide them.  
Therefore, we must understand that they committed the historical sin of killing the Messiah by misinterpreting the Old Testament.  
Just as only the CIA director can decipher the code, only God knows how to interpret the Bible. However, to fulfill God's will, God must teach in advance and teach again when the time comes... If we look at Amos 3:7, it says, "Surely the Lord God does nothing unless He reveals His secret to His servants the prophets."  
Therefore, we must recognize that those who believed in the Old Testament committed the historical sin of misinterpreting it and killing the Messiah. The Jewish believers at that time were still better. Jesus, who claims John the Baptist is Elijah, is doing extraordinary things. He performs miraculous signs and does many strange things throughout history, so they cannot deny or affirm it. They say, "If he claims John the Baptist is Elijah, then if Elijah has come, it will be resolved; if Elijah has not come... then let's ask." Thus, a public debate arose.  
The issue is found in John 1:19 and following. Look it up. "Are you the Coming One, or do we look for another?" When they asked, he denied it all. Even if he was not Elijah, he should have emphasized that John the Baptist was one of the prophets. But he denied it all.  
Why did that happen? Even though the Israelites believed he was a prophet, why did he deny it? The situation had already become unfavorable. He had become the Jesus who was being rejected by the nation and the church, and now it was clear what Jesus was saying. When the Jewish people and the Pharisees saw the situation and were trying to catch and kill him, it became a big deal. John the Baptist, who could not represent heaven from a human perspective, denied that he was even one of the prophets. So at that time, would they believe Jesus' words or John the Baptist's words? If a young person came out in America and said, "Billy Graham is Elijah, and I am Jesus," would you believe that?  
In the midst of this historical confusion, God sent the one Messiah, Jesus Christ, whom He had prepared for 4,000 years, to this nation with hope, yet this nation, in its ignorance, disbelieved and killed Him.  
314   A New Future for Christianity  
Is that true or not? Let's find out through the apostles of the New Testament. At that time, the Jews and the entire nation of Israel tried to kill Jesus, but who was the main instigator and representative in that killing? It was Apostle Paul. He not only killed Jesus but also tried to kill His disciples. On the way to Damascus, he was struck down and turned back to God, repenting and testifying. Apostle Paul, more than anyone, knew what happened to Jesus, and he boldly proclaimed in 1 Corinthians 2:8, "None of the rulers of this age knew; for had they known, they would not have crucified the Lord of glory." There is no way to deny this.  
How tragic it is that the Lord who came had to walk the path of the cross, something we have not even thought about, but have blindly believed. Even though Jesus, who should not have died, died, we believed He came to die. This is historically... So how can we go before Jesus? Even if we are saved, do we have the confidence to meet Him?  
Because of John the Baptist's mistake, Jesus died.  
The Jews could surely kill Jesus because they believed in the Old Testament... But what about John the Baptist? If you look at Matthew 11:2 and go down, when John the Baptist was imprisoned and about to die due to Herodias' affair, he sent two of his disciples to ask Jesus, "Are You the Coming One, or do we look for another?" Did John the Baptist believe or not? At one time, he testified before a large crowd by the Jordan River, saying, "Behold the Lamb of God who takes away the sin of the world." How could he send people to ask, "Are You the Coming One, or should we wait for another?"  
Consider how shocking it must have been for him to ask, when there was not a single person in the world who recognized him, and the entire church and nation opposed him, yet he, who had hoped for life as a lifeline, came to the end and asked, "Is He the Messiah or not?"  
So in verse 6, he says, "Blessed is he who is not offended because of Me," indicating that he had already sinned.  
Then in verse 7, when John the Baptist testified about Jesus by the Jordan River, he sarcastically hit his disciples with what the crowd had all heard and seen. He asked, "What did you go out to see in the wilderness? A reed shaken by the wind? But what did you go out to see? A man clothed in soft garments? Indeed, those who wear soft clothing are in kings' houses." This was a sarcastic attack.  
And in verse 11, he said, "Among those born of women, there has not risen one greater than John the Baptist; but he who is least in the kingdom of heaven is greater than he." How could he say such contradictory words? All the prophets who have gone to that kingdom were born of women, right? Did they come out from between stones? They were all born of women. If he was born of a woman, then John the Baptist should also be great in that kingdom, so why is he considered small?  
The reason is that the prophets who came in the past and are now in that kingdom testified about the Messiah from a distance and with historical distance, but John the Baptist, being sent as a prophet, had to testify directly about the Messiah, so he could only be the greatest.  
However, why did he say that the least in heaven is greater than he? Because even the least prophet in the spiritual realm knows that Jesus Christ is the Messiah and serves Him, but John the Baptist, who testified about Jesus, did not serve Him properly, so he could only be a mere footnote. We must understand that this is the content of His words.  
Let's look further down. Let's see if this is true in verse 12. "From the days of John the Baptist until now, the kingdom of heaven suffers violence, and the violent take it by force," indicating that there could be a struggle to seize the kingdom of heaven between Jesus and John the Baptist.  
316   A New Future for Christianity  
What this means is that John the Baptist did not strive for his mission. We need to understand what would have happened if John the Baptist had strived. If he had, he would have become the chief disciple.  
If John the Baptist had become the chief disciple, his disciples would have been the twelve apostles, and those following John the Baptist would have become seventy or even one hundred and twenty, and all the loyal subjects of the Jewish nation would have joined Jesus' group.  
Was John the Baptist sent to testify to oppose Jesus? So then, let’s find out how great John the Baptist was. How special was he, recognized by God and sent? Let’s look at Jesus' words. In verse 13, He said, "For all the prophets and the law prophesied until John." Jesus proclaimed that he came as a fruitful existence that completes the Old Testament. If John the Baptist had united with Jesus, all those who believed in the Old Testament and the Jewish scriptures would have followed and united. If that had happened, who would have killed Jesus?  
The Messiah, the Son of God, came to utilize the foundation laid down, not to feed unworthy fishermen, prostitutes, and tax collectors and become their master or teacher.  
Now, did they follow Jesus or not? Let’s confirm that once again. In John 3:26 and following, when John the Baptist's disciples spoke about Jesus, saying, "Rabbi, He who was with You beyond the Jordan, to whom You have testified, behold, He is baptizing, and all are coming to Him," John the Baptist replied, "He must increase, but I must decrease." The established church interprets this as "John the Baptist was a great prophet, so he elevated Jesus and said he would decrease."  
After struggling for three years for the Messiah he hoped for, if he had met and testified about that Messiah, he should have died for the Messiah. This means that if they had worked together, if the Messiah increased, he would also increase, and if the Messiah decreased, he would also decrease. The fact that they went in two different directions is a decisive acknowledgment of not following.  
317  
In this way, we have not realized until now that Jesus went to the cross because of the Old Testament and because of John the Baptist.  
The Lord does not come riding on clouds.  
Next, let's understand the third reason. At that time, the Jewish people believed that the coming Messiah would come riding on clouds. Why? Because it is prophesied in Daniel 7:13, "One like the Son of Man, coming with the clouds of heaven..." Those who take the Old Testament as life could not help but believe He would come on clouds.  
Here, some pastors might say, "That statement might be misunderstood by Reverend Moon. That statement refers to the second coming, not the time of Jesus..." But absolutely not! According to Jesus' words, it all ended at the time of John the Baptist. The Old Testament, all prophecies, and all prophets ended with John the Baptist.  
They expected Him to come on clouds, but could the one born of a woman, the son of Mary and Joseph, who everyone knew, qualify to be the Messiah? If Christians believe the Lord will come on clouds, would they believe He came as a person? It is the same. Now, let’s see if this was an issue in the apostolic age through the Bible. In 2 John 7, it says, "For many deceivers have gone out into the world who do not confess Jesus Christ as coming in the flesh. This is a deceiver and an antichrist." This is the problem.  
What this means is that today, when Christians believe the Lord will come on clouds, if He comes as a person, they oppose that person, and he is like an antichrist. There is no way to excuse this. What I am saying is entirely based on the Bible you believe. Because I love God's will more than anyone and want to walk the path of God's will correctly, I cannot help but say these things before you. You may ask, "What authority does Reverend Moon have to speak?" But I have the authority to say such things. I have met Jesus and John the Baptist, and it turned out this way, and I found it in the Bible. Both sides match, so it must be true. You can talk globally through Telstar. Is what you believed correct, or is what Reverend Moon said correct? Even if you, who are here, do not believe, your children will surely believe.  
When we see this, even though Jesus did not come to die, the fact that He ended up dying is God's sorrow, the sorrow of Judaism, the sorrow of humanity, the historical sorrow, and the sorrow of the future. We have not realized this until now.  
The place where He died on the cross is the place where everything was lost.  
We must understand that the Old Testament prophesied in two ways that the Messiah would come. If we look at Isaiah 9, 12, and 60, it says He will appear as the glorious Lord, but in chapter 53, it prophesies that He will die on the cross. We must understand why there are dual prophecies like this.  
God is afraid of fallen humans, and Satan is afraid of them too. Why? Because they once believed fervently in God but then betrayed Him and conspired with Satan to ruin God's world, and then, having united with Satan, they came to God to ruin the world of Satan. That is why both God and Satan are afraid.  
If they had believed, they would have become the glorious Lord, but because they did not believe, they ended up on the cross. We must understand that the cross was a sudden event. Now, when was the decision made for Him to go to the cross? Let’s find out through the Bible.  
In Luke 9:30, it says, "Suddenly, two men talked with Him, who were Moses and Elijah, who appeared in glory and spoke of His decease which He was about to accomplish at Jerusalem." It was decided on the Mount of Transfiguration.  
319  
Because Judaism opposed Him, the nation of Israel was in such a state, and even John the Baptist stood in opposition, the foundation to fulfill the will was already all destroyed. Therefore, God could not do anything, so He abandoned the dual providence and, centering on spirit and flesh, intended to complete salvation in the spiritual realm, cutting off the physical world and paving the way for the cross. If He did not go to the cross, He would lose both aspects. He had no choice but to give Jesus to the cross to leave at least one aspect.  
Today, Christians claim that Jesus definitely came to die based on Matthew 16:22-23. What does that verse say?
When Peter spoke about Jesus going to Jerusalem to die, he said, "Oh, teacher, please don't do that." At that moment, Jesus rebuked him, saying, "Get behind me, Satan." Therefore, Christians think, "Jesus, who came to die, was opposed by Peter, so he called him Satan." However, you must clearly understand that this response could not be avoided since Jesus had already decided to return to the cross on the Mount of Transfiguration.

What if John the Baptist, the Jews, and the people of Israel had believed in Jesus? The people of Israel would have united with Jesus. If that had happened, even the Arab world would have united with Jesus. With this, within 40 years, they would have drawn all of Rome to the side of heaven. The dead Jesus conquered Rome over 400 years, so centered around the living Jesus, they would have proclaimed the constitution of the heavenly kingdom within 40 years. If that had happened, there would be no Christianity or Catholicism today. Everything would have unfolded from the position of the people of Israel. If this had been the case, the people of Israel would not have faced such a miserable downfall in the Middle East, and Christians would not have suffered and shed blood. By unifying royal authority, Christianity could have moved the world; who would have killed him?

If that had happened, the world would have already been in accordance with the will of Jesus, and the world would have been completely fulfilled. There would be no need for the Lord to return. Why would he come back? Christianity must understand this.

Therefore, we must recognize that the place where Jesus died on the cross is the place where God and Jesus lost everything. The cross is not God's victory, but the victory of Satan. It is the place where the Son of God was captured and crucified.

For this reason, losing the nation of Israel, losing the Jews, losing the schedule of world history, losing all the apostles, and ultimately even losing the thief on the right side happened at the cross. There is no Christianity there. There is no starting point for Christianity. Everything was lost.

Where does Christianity begin? It began 40 days after Jesus resurrected. It is not the way of the cross but the way of resurrection that has been misunderstood until now. For 2,000 years, Christianity has fundamentally been teaching this. You cannot deny it when you look at the Bible. When Judas Iscariot came to arrest him, did he not say it was the hour of darkness?

If Jesus had come to die, would he have prayed three times in the Garden of Gethsemane, saying, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as you will"? (Matthew 26:39) Such a prayer would disqualify him as the Messiah. You must understand this.

Why did he pray like that? Was it because he was afraid of dying? Christians say, "Oh, Jesus had a physical body, so he was in pain because of death." Not at all. It is not fear of death.

If he dies on the cross, all Christians around the world must follow the way of the cross, and because of his shedding of blood, the condition is established for Satan to trample upon the bodies of Christians worldwide. When he thinks of the countless people who will shed blood and sacrifice, he could not help but pray like that. Also, seeing that the nation of Israel and Judaism, which had been prepared for 4,000 years, were all collapsing and losing their foundation, when he thought of the labor God had put in for 4,000 years, he could not help but pray like that.

Therefore, when Jesus finally died, he cried out, "My God, my God, why have you forsaken me?" What does this prayer mean?

We must understand that the three hours of darkness signify a time when the world is overtaken by the darkness that must be fulfilled before one will.

You have come to realize that the Messiah, who must fulfill the will without dying in the historical age, died like this.

Now, how will the Lord who is to come again come? There are dual prophecies in the New Testament, just like in the Old Testament. Today, Christians are in the same position as the Jews. The scope has only expanded globally.

However, Christianity is not about spirit and flesh but only spiritual. It has no nation. It does not have a national standard like the chosen people of Israel. Why? Because Jesus died. You must understand that it is not as good as the old Judaism. Jesus came as a spiritual king. Therefore, God's will is to save all humanity, expel Satan, and for God to become king. However, because Jesus died, he could not establish a kingdom on earth where he could rule, so the Messiah must come again to fulfill that will. Thus, for all Christians around the world to unite around the coming Lord and establish the kingdom of heaven on earth, a strong nation must be created that surpasses the failures of the ancient people of Israel.

In Revelation 1:7, it is prophesied that the Lord will come on the clouds. In 1 Thessalonians 5:2, it says he will come like a thief. Now, how can he come on the clouds and also come like a thief? Can you decide to believe in the Lord who comes on the clouds and not believe in the Lord who comes like a thief? Believing in the Lord who comes on the clouds is the same as believing that Elijah and the Messiah will come on the clouds; if he comes as a person, it means he comes like a thief.

When we look at how God worked during the Old Testament era, do you think Jesus will come on the clouds? If you believe that, they will kill him again. The people who believe in Jesus will kill the one who comes.

We must believe in both sides of the prophecy. The Bible says so, so we must believe. He can come on the clouds and also come as a person. If you believe he will come on the clouds, you might kill him if he comes as a person, but if you believe he will come as a person and he comes on the clouds, you will surely welcome him.

In Revelation 12:5, it says, "She bore a male child who will rule all the nations with a rod of iron." It says that a woman gives birth. The church could not accept this, so it has interpreted it as him coming on the clouds until now. Then, let’s see how many things do not come to pass if he comes on the clouds. Look at Luke 17:20 and following. "When the Pharisees asked when the kingdom of God would come, Jesus answered them, 'The kingdom of God does not come with observation.'" Can you not see him coming on the clouds? Is there no sign? Then, in verse 22, it says, "The days will come when you will desire to see one of the days of the Son of Man, and you will not see it." Can you not see him coming on the clouds? This is what the Bible says. In verse 25, it says, "But first he must suffer many things and be rejected by this generation." Does the Lord who comes on the clouds suffer? Is it as tragic as in the days of Noah? If he comes as a person, this is what will happen. If he comes as a person, it will definitely be like this.

If all Christians around the world expect him to come on the clouds, but he comes as a person, will not the Pope and all those with a strong base in power try to kill the heretics who ruin Christianity and God's will? Wouldn't they? The Bible says so.

When we look at historical facts, we must naturally conclude that God is alive here, and we can find that God's will is intentional and official.

Mr. Moon appears here and teaches these things diligently; if there were no one to teach, they would kill him again. Is there any way around it? They would kill him again. The time has come. If Reverend Moon does not say these things, can you guarantee that you will not do that?

Then, in Luke 18:8, it says, "When the Son of Man comes, will he find faith on the earth?" This means there is no faith. They cannot even say the word faith. Can you not see faith when he comes on the clouds? They are believing like that… They are just like the Jews. They expected him to come on the clouds and for Elijah to come, but if he came as a person, would anyone believe? Were there any scribes or priests among the apostles of Jesus? Did anyone believe?

When we see these words, it is the Bible that says that if he comes on the clouds, these words will not come to pass.

Christianity must welcome the Lord who comes as a person.

I want to ask you one thing: What is God's will? Does he want to be the God of a Christian denomination, or does he want to be the God of humanity? God's will is to become the God of all humanity. The Savior did not come just to save Christianity. You must understand that he came to save the world.

As you well know, in John 3:16, it says, "For God so loved the world that he gave his only begotten Son, that whoever believes in him should not perish but have everlasting life." It does not say he loved one denomination or one individual. It says he loved the world. So, has the whole world found this God? Has it expelled Satan? Where did it get lost? It got lost on earth, so it must come to find it on earth.

Therefore, in Matthew 16:19, when Jesus gave the keys of the kingdom to Peter, he said, "Whatever you bind on earth will be bound in heaven." He emphasized that the earth is important. Everything must be resolved on earth.

So, has God established his kingdom on earth, governing all humanity? Is Satan holding the royal authority? If not, God cannot fulfill his plan, and God becomes a God who fails. If the plan is turned around, God becomes a God who fails. Who is to blame? It is Satan. Therefore, the conclusion is that Satan is the only one who cannot do it. That is why in Isaiah 46:11, it says, "I have spoken, and I will bring it to pass; I have purposed, and I will do it."

Let us conclude. We have the ancestry of evil humanity, the origin of evil couples, and the origin of evil brothers. Because we have not been able to give birth to sinless sons and daughters with true ancestors, true couples, and true brothers of good humanity, you must understand that this must be fulfilled on earth.

Therefore, if we do not find a family centered on God, we cannot find a nation or the world. That is why Jesus came to this earth to establish a family loved by God. In other words, centered on a man who must find a bride as a groom, true parents, true couples, and true brothers can emerge. Because this has not been decisively fulfilled, it has been prophesied that he will come again to accomplish this, which is the wedding feast of the Lamb, where the groom meets the bride. We must have a family to find a tribe, a nation, and the world, so the family is the issue. You must understand that the wedding feast of the Lamb is about the groom and bride meeting. God must fulfill the alpha of the will that should have been achieved when there was no fall, circle back, remove the evil world, and align it with the omega.

The first Adam failed, and the second Adam, Jesus, must restore that, but because he could not do that, he must come again in the third coming. The reason it says in 1 Corinthians 15:45 that Jesus is the second Adam is because of this.

You must understand that he could not accomplish everything by coming on the clouds; he must come as a person. Therefore, centered on the true ancestors of humanity, true couples, and the new Christianity, we must be grafted in and create the royal authority of the world to fulfill the kingdom of heaven. This is the mission of Christianity to welcome the coming Lord.

Now, knowing that such a time is approaching us, I hope you can participate in such a place through your prayers. I appreciate the message I shared with you this evening, and I ask you not to jump to conclusions but to seek resolution before God through prayer. Thank you.
